misticos: –Ω–∞–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–µ

misticos: —ä—É—ä update

misticos: The Linux client is retired this patch. You will no longer be able to play Rust natively on Linux.

–°–∞—à–∞: –ö–∞–µ—Ñ

misticos: Our client now uses IL2CPP. Unity claims this helps with performance and makes the code harder to decompile

misticos: For the server things are a bit more complicated since we don't want to break existing mods. Due to this we've decided to keep Mono the default for the server and ship IL2CPP on a separate, optional branch

misticos: Workshop Skin Compression. This greatly reduces the game install size (by about 8GB) and lessens the impact future skin releases have on the update download size. Note that this does not affect RAM usage as crunch texture compression is only applied on disk, not in memory.

misticos: - Horse equipment: Shoes, bags (= storage), etc. - Tesla coil: Damage players with electricity! - Simple sight is a default blueprint now. - Basic ammunition information (like for food) in inventory UI. - Exploit fixes: No lerp convar, disarming landmines from any distance, free underwater loot crates from any distance, interaction with excavator from any distance. - Map: Place marker by right clicking, you'll see it on an in-game compass. Appears on your teammates map and compass if you're a team leader. Remove the marker by right clicking it. Added a death marker. - New death screen: See and select bags on the map, see the map with your teammates' positions, group sleeping bags, etc. - Screen settings: Fullscreen exclusive, Fullscreen Borderless, Windowed. Also a FPS limit slider. Use Apply Changes to apply them. - Rotate your character in inventory UI. - Crafting: Favorites (Hover -> Press star), 0.75 cooldown between quick craft list update and craft click, right click item in the queue to move it to the start, right click quick craft icon to remove from queue, middle click quick craft to add x5 to crafting queue (or less if cant afford), favorites category, electrical category. - Items splitting: Right click split bar to type an exact amount, shift-middle mouse drag to split a third of a stack, middle/shirt-middle click the splitter to set it to half/third.  Admins QoL: - Godmode: No status effects, no food and hydration depletion, no radiation poisoning.  New commands: - headlerp: Adjust head snapback speed after alt look. - headlerp_inertia: Smooth the head snapback motion after alt look. - refillvitals: Refill health, calories and hydration. - heal: Just like hurt with negative values. - grass.distance: Set grass draw distance.  Weapons changes: - Spas-12: Fire rate increased - M92: Fire rate decreased - M39: Available at Bandit Town - L96: Removed from Bandit Town - Shotgun Slugs: More accurate, more damage, closer damage falloff

misticos: - Repair QoL: Messages with a reason about repairing failure. - Quick item drop (single/stack) with specific binds in Controls (no default). - OilRig: Removed recyclers, military and elite crates are only behind keycard puzzles, no easily accessible keycards, reduced loot spawns overall. - Sounds: New bear sounds, softened up ambient sounds and foliage rustles, polished up collectible item pickup sounds, new pressure pad sounds, heli rotors attacks are louder and have less volume fluctuation, barefoot footsteps are lighter and less harsh in the high end. - Excavator buff: 5000 (+2000) stone, 750 (+250) sulfur, or 2000 (+500) metal fragments.
